[09:35:06.455]                   muffleCondition <- function (cond, pattern = "^muffle") 
[09:35:06.455]                   {
[09:35:06.455]                     inherits <- base::inherits
[09:35:06.455]                     invokeRestart <- base::invokeRestart
[09:35:06.455]                     is.null <- base::is.null
[09:35:06.455]                     muffled <- FALSE
[09:35:06.455]                     if (inherits(cond, "message")) {
[09:35:06.455]                       muffled <- grepl(pattern, "muffleMessage")
[09:35:06.455]                       if (muffled) 
[09:35:06.455]                         invokeRestart("muffleMessage")
[09:35:06.455]                     }
[09:35:06.455]                     else if (inherits(cond, "warning")) {
[09:35:06.455]                       muffled <- grepl(pattern, "muffleWarning")
[09:35:06.455]                       if (muffled) 
[09:35:06.455]                         invokeRestart("muffleWarning")
[09:35:06.455]                     }
[09:35:06.455]                     else if (inherits(cond, "condition")) {
[09:35:06.455]                       if (!is.null(pattern)) {
[09:35:06.455]                         computeRestarts <- base::computeRestarts
[09:35:06.455]                         grepl <- base::grepl
[09:35:06.455]                         restarts <- computeRestarts(cond)
[09:35:06.455]                         for (restart in restarts) {
[09:35:06.455]                           name <- restart$name
[09:35:06.455]                           if (is.null(name))
